 บ  Dear RCN,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The scene seems to be rampant with traders with big egos and          บ
 บ  attitudes.  Some veteran traders just smile and express that the scene    บ
 บ  would be dead if it weren't for the ego that drives traders and groups    บ
 บ  to do their best.  I think it's time to put this to debate and place it   บ
 บ  in its proper terms.  There are some traders who brag and act like they   บ
 บ  are 'the shit' 101% of the time.  These poor souls usually end up         บ
 บ  getting in trouble and getting kicked out of groups when they shoot       บ
 บ  their mouths off.  Other traders who are experienced know they are among  บ
 บ  the best.                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Traders who say they are the best and can back it up on a             บ
 บ  consistently shouldn't be called egotistic if they keep bragging to an    บ
 บ  acceptable level.  Some traders are good and they brag to excess.  These  บ
 บ  people usually have problems eventually when they cross another trader    บ
 บ  who can waste them on a site or board.  Those who seem to make a big      บ
 บ  deal about having some pride need to chill.  Everyone who sacrifices      บ
 บ  5-14 hours a day in the scene deserves some recognition when they do a    บ
 บ  good job.  If they act like assholes by taking their boasts to extremes   บ
 บ  just laugh and know that they will fuck themselves over eventually.       บ
 บ  They are their own worst enemy.  They will get theirs in the end.  The    บ
 บ  scene is driven by ego to some extent, since no sane person would invest  บ
 บ  the time and effort we all do just to get a few games and utils that      บ
 บ  actually work and are worth downloading.                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      If someone starts to act like an asshole in a channel then just tell  บ
 บ  him to fuck off and get a girlfriend.  Don't make a big deal out of       บ
 บ  their huge ego.  Other people will notice and will hurt the trader        บ
 บ  eventually.  If they are just idly bragging in the channel how they       บ
 บ  cranked a board and they aren't talking like they are the only good       บ
 บ  trader in the channel, jut say 'good job.'  Don't get all uptight when    บ
 บ  someone discusses his accomplishments.  Just go with it and don't whine.  บ
 บ  I'm kinda sick of people whining that this trader or that trader is an    บ
 บ  egotistical bastard.  We all are to some degree.  Don't condemn a bit of  บ
 บ  bragging because we all do it.  If the trader acts like an asshole then   บ
 บ  just sit back and lugh while he is making himself look like a fool.       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Defender Zeta             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Reporter : Super Hacker              Interviewee : <Undisclosed>        บ
 บ    Subject  : RCMP, April 2, 1996       Affiliation : <Undisclosed>        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : When and how were you busted and for what?                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  UND : On April 2nd, 1996 the RCMP "Royal Canadian Mounted Police" raided  บ
 บ        my house and confiscated over $25,000 worth of computer equipment.  บ
 บ        The warrant said "Copyright Infringment".  Their plan is to         บ
 บ        completely eradicate software piracy off of the Internet by the     บ
 บ        year 1997; and they are well equiped to do just that.  I know for   บ
 บ        a fact that many members of the different groups over the past      บ
 บ        year are in fact Microsoft agents working on this investigation.    บ
 บ        They will definitely take out anyone they want.  I mean, who are    บ
 บ        we kidding here...                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Sice September of last year, Microsoft, IBM, Lotus, Core, Autodes,  บ
 บ        and a few other companies have worked together in an "Internet      บ
 บ        Anti-Piracy Campaign".  They have been working undercover in the    บ
 บ        warez scene collecting information about the  various groups and    บ
 บ        their respective members.  They would seek out information such as  บ
 บ        who supplies and who couriers, etc.  In your opinion, is the warez  บ
 บ        scene not to be as trusted as before, and that even you or I could  บ
 บ        be an undercover federal agent?                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  UND : Absolutely.  How can you even think of trusting someone you will    บ
 บ        never in your life met.  I mean, a handle could be anyone; it       บ
 บ        could even be Bill Gates you're trading the newest build of         บ
 บ        Windows NT with.  How  can you know for sure who you're talking     บ
 บ        to.  It is just not worth it.  I could be looking at up too         บ
 บ        $25,000 in fines and/or 8 months in jail for every offense!         บ
 บ        That's every ware!  That's insane!  And all these lamers on IRC     บ
 บ        who say "Oh, the feds don't care about courier groups, it's all     บ
 บ        bullshit!  Distributing copyrighted software is just as bad if not  บ
 บ        worse than the person who supplied it in the first place.  The      บ
 บ        supplier gives it to one person.  The couriers give it to           บ
 บ        thousands of people! How would you know if I am a federal agent or  บ
 บ        not, and how would I know if you're not.  It's simple, the          บ
 บ        Internet is an imaginary world, where people can be whatever they   บ
 บ        want.  The federal agents who are working with Microsoft are        บ
 บ        taking advantage of that.  There's no such thing as entrapment on   บ
 บ        the Internet.  They don't have to tell you jack.  In fact, about    บ
 บ        99% of all narqs are not federal agents.  They are usually just     บ
 บ        students or Microsoft employees.  The federal agents are just the   บ
 บ        guys who take the information these people hand them and then go    บ
 บ        kick in your door.  They just pick up the scraps when Microsoft     บ
 บ        has enough information on you.                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : How long have you being in the scene?  And in your opinion, do you  บ
 บ        see the scene dying out as many veterans are starting to leave the  บ
 บ        scene?                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  UND : I've been a major part of the scene ever since the C64 days.  And   บ
 บ        as far as I am concerned, the scene is all but dead now.  I mean,   บ
 บ        there are a lot of great people left, but how can you possibly      บ
 บ        hide from these huge companies?  If you have half a brain, you'd    บ
 บ        get out of the scene before these companies get you.  It's just     บ
 บ        not worth it.  I would that couriers are in EVEN bigger shit than   บ
 บ        suppliers.  From my observations, they apparently don't really      บ
 บ        care about the games scene.  It's the utils they are after in a     บ
 บ        big way by companies such as Microsoft, IBM, etc. All the big time  บ
 บ        elite dudes I used to know have either retired, or have been        บ
 บ        busted by now.  With all these new people coming in, I would say    บ
 บ        that 2 out of every 10 work in some way with Microsoft, the SPA,    บ
 บ        or some other government agency.  It's just not fair, we can't      บ
 บ        win...                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What happened on the day you of your bust?  Did they let you go?    บ
 บ        Did they confiscate anything?                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  UND : I was out of town on business.  They came to my house, kicked in    บ
 บ        the door and confiscated everything that had anything to do with    บ
 บ        computers, all my systems, monitors, cables, books, notepads,       บ
 บ        scribble pads, scraps of paper, etc.  If you walked in right after  บ
 บ        they left.  You would have no clue that I had anything to do with   บ
 บ        computers.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Did they charge you with a crime?  Did they take you to jail?       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  UND : I was not arrested. And I still have not been charged with          บ
 บ        anything.  They are going through my systems with a fine toothed    บ
 บ        comb as we speak...                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Did you have a lot of pirated software on your system?              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  UND : Well I am not really in a position to say.  Who knows who will be   บ
 บ        reading this.  I will say that I considered myself untouchable for  บ
 บ        the longest time.  I mean, I always heard of people getting busted  บ
 บ        and I was always said, "Oh shit, that guy's screwed."  But it was   บ
 บ        never supposed to happen to me.  It's like something you watch on   บ
 บ        television.  But I'll tell you this.  I was one of the most         บ
 บ        careful people out there and they got me.  That means they can get  บ
 บ        anyone, anytime, anywhere.  No questions asked.  Whenever I see     บ
 บ        people saying, "Oh they'll never get me, or I'm not worried.  I     บ
 บ        think they're idiots, PERIOD.  It's simple, Microsoft's gang is     บ
 บ        bigger than the scene, more well equipped and more experienced.     บ
 บ        The scene is outmatched.                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Do you have any idea or any information of the person that narqed   บ
 บ        on you?  Is there someone you suspect (I remind you that your       บ
 บ        handle will not be mentioned in this interview)?                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  UND : I know for a fact that someone narqued on me.  I thought I knew     บ
 บ        who it was.  But after talking with this person, I realized that    บ
 บ        it could have been any one of about 8 different people in that      บ
 บ        area.  When I hit court, I will find out for sure.  When I do,      บ
 บ        EVERYONE will know who the narq was.  Mark my words on that one...  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : And you will personally inform RCN who this person is?              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  UND : Of course, RCN is the most widely read E-Zine.  I have no problem   บ
 บ        with that.  I go by the code of the scene which is to never NARQ    บ
 บ        on anyone under any circumstances.  The person who narqued on me    บ
 บ        is a fucking low-life piece of shit.  I will find out who he is,    บ
 บ        and when I do, EVERYONE in the scene will know.  I promise you      บ
 บ        that.                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : I have known you for a very long time and you basically set me up   บ
 บ        with most of the groups I am in today.  What do you suggest for     บ
 บ        people out in scene in how we can protect ourselves?  Don't         บ
 บ        federal agents need a warrant to break into a house?                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  UND : Yes, they need a warrant.  However, the Microsoft anti-piracy team  บ
 บ        is very respected and can easily get a warrant from the             บ
 บ        government.  I suggest that if you belong to a group.  No matter    บ
 บ        how big or how small, that you absolutely make sure that you do     บ
 บ        not have a single piece of copyrighted file on your system.  Don't  บ
 บ        even keep a record of anything regarding the scene.  If you need    บ
 บ        to get on IRC, use a shell account, preferably a hacked one.  Buy   บ
 บ        all your software, from the store!  If you belong to a group, make  บ
 บ        your system 100% legitimate.  Because when they come, and they      บ
 บ        will, the slightest little scrap of information that tie you to a   บ
 บ        group, or to the scene in anyway could make the difference you      บ
 บ        walking away or getting convicted!                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Do you think groups such as Razor 1911, which have been around for  บ
 บ        about 25+ years would be able to survive in the scene?              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  UND : No groups have been around for 25 years.  There are no groups that  บ
 บ        are immune to this.  Anyone in the scene is fair game to these      บ
 บ        guys.  They are probably not interested in groups like Razor since  บ
 บ        it's a games group.  They are more interested in groups that        บ
 บ        specialize in utils, like DOD and PWA.  But when it comes right     บ
 บ        down to it.  I think they just want to clean us all right off the   บ
 บ        face of the Internet.  I would say it's a fair bet that every       บ
 บ        single group in the scene at this point in time has at least 1 or   บ
 บ        2 members that are a part of Microsoft's anti-piracy team, as       บ
 บ        members of these groups, I would bet my life on that.  I don't      บ
 บ        trust anyone anymore.  As I have said, it could be anyone you are   บ
 บ        talking to.                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : That is true, but what about users who are in Africa?  I'll be      บ
 บ        moving to Africa in 2 weeks.  There are no piracy laws there, and   บ
 บ        they're not going to bust anyone there.                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  UND : Well I wouldn't know about the laws in Africa, but I do know that   บ
 บ        in Canada and the U.S., you're screwed if they catch you.  In       บ
 บ        Canada, the maximum penalties by law for copyright infringment is   บ
 บ        $25,000 in fine and/or 8 months in jail, per offense.  In the       บ
 บ        U.S., it's up to a million in fines, and up to 5 years in jail!!!   บ
 บ        And that information is right out of my lawyer's mouth.  It's no    บ
 บ        joke, this is very serious shit.  All I have to say is this, I      บ
 บ        hope people listen.  I am not some punk.  I have been around for    บ
 บ        many years now, and what I'm seeing now is not good for the scene.  บ
 บ        The federal agents are definitely coming in full force.  People     บ
 บ        are dropping like flies and they are not going to stop untio they   บ
 บ        get the results they want.  This scares me.  However, the few       บ
 บ        people in the scene whom I actually consider personal friends       บ
 บ        "outside the scene" have listened to me, and have gotten out, I     บ
 บ        hope.  I will always be around, I have just stopped the             บ
 บ        downloading and spreading.  It's not worth it.  My friends know     บ
 บ        who I am, and they will always be my friends.                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : I really appreciate this interview, and on the behalf of RCN, we    บ
 บ        would like to thank you for letting us conduct it.  We know how     บ
 บ        hard it is and it is very scary to get busted, especially since     บ
 บ        you are married and have 4 kids, and have to go to jail for         บ
 บ        copyright infringement.  I hope everything works out for you.       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  UND : Thanks man, I will keep RCN informed on what's going on...          บ

 บ    Reporter : Rebel Chicken             Interviewee : Tsunami              บ
 บ    Subject  : Tsunami *BUSTED*          Affiliation : Ex-fATE Courier      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : You recently left the warez scene for a few months, you seemed to   บ
 บ        have just disappeared, was there a reason why?                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  TSU : I got busted.  Actually for all the warez I was pirating, I got     บ
 บ        busted for something I didn't do.  I was using a "shared" account   บ
 บ        at Sydney University.  Unbeknownst to me, there were a lot of       บ
 บ        other people using the same account, and a few of those people      บ
 บ        decided to hack a U.S. missile base, and they were actually quite   บ
 บ        successful at their little venture.                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : They hacked into the U.S. MISSILE BASE???  What the hell were they  บ
 บ        trying to do, launch some nukes and start World War III?..          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  TSU : I know, they were pathetically stupid, I mean that's ASKING to be   บ
 บ        caught, but, they are in a LOT of trouble now (tee hee).  This      บ
 บ        wasn't some sort of mini warez thing, so the U.S. government        บ
 บ        decided to ring our Australian federal agents and then they called  บ
 บ        AusCERT (Australian Computer Emergency Response Team) and they      บ
 บ        traced calls to and from the Sydney University accounts.  That's    บ
 บ        where I was stuffed, I found all my Sydney University accounts      บ
 บ        cancelled and they took me in for an "interview".  Argh, they       บ
 บ        taped in TRIPLICATE...                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What's a triplicate?                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  TSU : The AusCERT taped the interview onto three tapes simultaneously.    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Yikes, so the AusCert found you by tracing your phoneline?          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  TSU : Yes, looks like it, that could have been the only way.              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Do you remember what kind of questions they asked you in the        บ
 บ        "interview"?  What were they trying to find out?                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  TSU : They were asking me if I knew how to create shell script programs,  บ
 บ        why I was using the account, who gave me the account, and why the   บ
 บ        account was used for hacking the U.S. missile base.                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Hacking into a U.S. missile base is a little more eye-catching      บ
 บ        than carding a fake account.  After you were interviewed, did you   บ
 บ        immediately come back into the warez scene?  If not, how long was   บ
 บ        it before you decided to come back to the scene?                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  TSU : Immediately?  Shit no, I haven't been online since they took away   บ
 บ        computer, and I no longer have Internet access, but I hope to have  บ
 บ        my computer back soon.. a few weeks at most, MAYBE...               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : They took away your computer?  How are you chatting with me right   บ
 บ        now?  You're not chatting with me on an AusCERT computer terminal,  บ
 บ        are you?  If they didn't charge you with anything like hacking,     บ
 บ        how could they have confiscated your computer?  Don't they need to  บ
 บ        have "just cause" and "due process" before they have the right to   บ
 บ        confiscate private property?                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  TSU : Well, they COULD charge me with unlawful access and a bunch of      บ
 บ        shit, so I really didn't want to argue with them when they came     บ
 บ        and took it.  I'm currently using a friends account at New Castle   บ
 บ        University, 2 hours north of Sydney.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Do you think it's SAFE for you to come back to the scene?  Since    บ
 บ        your interview with the AusCERT, do you feel that it might have an  บ
 บ        adverse effect on the groups you were affiliated with?  For         บ
 บ        example, it is well known that you are a great courier for a great  บ
 บ        courier group, fATE (Fast Action Trade Exchange), did the AusCERT   บ
 บ        dig deep into your warez habits, or did they skip over anything     บ
 บ        related to warez?  In other words, did they care that you were      บ
 บ        pirating, or were they only interested in the hackers?              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  TSU : A stroke of luck for me was that they were only interested in the   บ
 บ        hackers, and since I'm not into hacking, warez was never part of    บ
 บ        the big picture.  I'm trying to lay low for a while (Woops,         บ
 บ        granting an interview to the most read E-Mag in the scene is not a  บ
 บ        good way to lay low *slap* do'h).                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Do you have any names/handles of those who were actually hacking    บ
 บ        the U.S. missile base?                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  TSU : Sorry, I don't want to get them into anymore trouble than what      บ
 บ        they are already in.  I decline to answer.                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Were you the only warez person using that account, or were there    บ
 บ        other more warez people using it?  HOW did you get accesss to that  บ
 บ        account in the first place?  Who gave you the account?  You         บ
 บ        obviously didn't pay for it.                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  TSU : How?  It was given to me by another "Netter" (Aren't they all?).    บ
 บ        I was the main warez person using the account since it was a dream  บ
 บ        account, unlimited quota.. woo wee...                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : The "Netter" who gave you the account, did he get interviewed by    บ
 บ        the Auscert as well?                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  TSU : Yes, he was one of the hackers.                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Ouch, guess he got a little more than just an interview.            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  TSU : He was stupid for doing it though, ruined me for a couple of        บ
 บ        months.                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  TSU : They confiscated my Pentium 120 MHz, 2 MEG Matrox Millenium, 24     บ
 บ        MEG RAM, 2 GIG HD, 15" monitor, SB16, 6x CD-ROM, and my Rhino 6     บ
 บ        motherboard :(                                                      บ

 บ  RCN : OUCHH...                                                            บ

 บ    Reporter : Rebel Chicken             Interviewee : David & Goliath      บ
 บ    Subject  : PWA+CORP=PWA              Affiliation : PWA Senior Member    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : The Corporation was capable of showing the scene that it was a      บ
 บ        very powerful release group even though the group was essentially   บ
 บ        very young.  The Corporation released quality utils on a regular    บ
 บ        basis, and as a result, the group became very well respected, and   บ
 บ        most considered The Corporation to be one of the top 3 utils        บ
 บ        groups comparable to PWA and DOD.  However, The Corporation         บ
 บ        recently merged into PWA, was this move an attempt to merge         บ
 บ        together the competiton?  The Corporation was good, but couldn't    บ
 บ        beat PWA, so The Corporation decides to join PWA?                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  D&G : The merge was basically put into effect because The Corporation     บ
 บ        was running into problems.  I became very busy, and the rest of     บ
 บ        the leaders/seniors did not have the time to run the group.  So we  บ
 บ        all looked at the different possibilities on what to do, and one    บ
 บ        thing that we all agreed on was that PWA was the #1 utils group;    บ
 บ        and that a merger with them would be beneficial to both groups.  I  บ
 บ        then contacted Snake about the merger and discovered that PWA was   บ
 บ        looking into something similar as well.                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : I agree with you, PWA is definitely the #1 utils group.  What will  บ
 บ        happen to the leaders/seniors of The Corporation?  After the        บ
 บ        merge, will they too become leaders/seniors of PWA, or will they    บ
 บ        be taken in as regular members?  How many The Corporation members   บ
 บ        were there at the time of the merge, and how many of those The      บ
 บ        Corporation members will make it into PWA?                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  D&G : Cyberjack and I have been made PWA Senior Members.  However, The    บ
 บ        Punisher left for Siege.  Vengeance is on vacation and has a        บ
 บ        member position, and Ustasa is also a member.  I don't have the     บ
 บ        exact figures of how many people from The Corporation made it into  บ
 บ        PWA, but a lot of inactive people were dropped, and only the best   บ
 บ        moved with us.                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : The Punisher went to Siege, a rival utils group?  Was The Punisher  บ
 บ        an important factor to The Corporation's release capabilities?      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  D&G : The Punisher is a great courier, and some consider him the best in  บ
 บ        the world.  His main duty in The Corporation was to organize the    บ
 บ        boards and couriers; and he did a great job at it when he had the   บ
 บ        time.  I believe that Siege will also be a major powerhouse since   บ
 บ        they have some great guys like Hemp Hoodlum, and Speed Master.      บ
 บ        And with time, they will become one of the top utils groups in the  บ
 บ        scene.                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Not only was The Corporation one of the top 3 utils groups, but it  บ
 บ        also had THE best board in the world.  The Corporation had Park     บ
 บ        Central as its WHQ, will Park Central become PWA's new WHQ?         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  D&G : Park Central will not be making the move.  Crackpot was very        บ
 บ        patient with us.  He took us in when we hadn't really proved        บ
 บ        ourselves, and helped us in many ways.  2 days before The           บ
 บ        Corporation merged with PWA, we had decided to take a break or      บ
 บ        something, that is until we could break the dry spell, and that's   บ
 บ        when Crackpot had decided to call it quits.  So Park Central will   บ
 บ        now be without a utils group, because that's the way he chooses to  บ
 บ        run his board.  Park Central will remain affiliated with RiSC and   บ
 บ        Dynamix.                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : WOO... Park Central is now open for a utils group, DOD perhaps?     บ
 บ        Anyways, I remember reading some messages on Park Central, and I    บ
 บ        could recall that Roland from DOD and you did NOT get along.  He    บ
 บ        posted messages about how lame this and that was, and how he was    บ
 บ        all this and that plus more.  Do you believe that perhaps now that  บ
 บ        The Corporation has merged into PWA, that Roland from DOD and or    บ
 บ        other members from DOD might show more resentment towards PWA,      บ
 บ        their #1 rival and competitor?  When the #1 (PWA) and #3 (Corp)     บ
 บ        utils groups merge, the number #2 (DOD) utils group, must show a    บ
 บ        little concern?                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  D&G : I doubt Park Central will be taking in any utils groups, but I      บ
 บ        can't say that for sure.  As for Roland, he and I shared our        บ
 บ        differences, but he is now no longer in the scene.  As far as DOD   บ
 บ        is concerned, I have not seen any resentment from them.  They have  บ
 บ        a great relationship with PWA, and ever since I have been there, I  บ
 บ        have seen no problems concerning the merge.                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : The DOD and PWA relationship is very admirable, and the smaller     บ
 บ        groups should learn to follow their example.  There's been a trend  บ
 บ        lately in which smaller groups merge into a bigger groups, ONLY to  บ
 บ        find out that a few months later, they merge back out.  For         บ
 บ        example, Scum merged into PWA when their leader, Liquidator, left   บ
 บ        the scene, however, once Liquidator came back to the scene, many    บ
 บ        of the old Scum members immediately left PWA and went straight      บ
 บ        back to Scum.   Do you feel that their might be a chance in the     บ
 บ        future in which The Corporation merges back out of PWA, or does it  บ
 บ        seem to be a PERMANENT merge (so far)?                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  D&G : I don't know the details about the whole Scum merge with PWA, but   บ
 บ        as far as I am concerned.  I want the PWA and The Corporation       บ
 บ        merge to be a permanent deal, and I hope in every regards that it   บ
 บ        will be. But it is hard to say what will really happen, but I will  บ
 บ        try 100% to make permanent.                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : BTW, Here's a personal question, I have a friend who's handle is    บ
 บ        Mike and Dave - and they happen to be two brothers, your handle is  บ
 บ        David and Goliath, are you one person or two people?                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  D&G : 2 people, and it's David & Goliath :)                               บ

 บ    Reporter : Super Hacker              Interviewee : Lester               บ
 บ    Subject  : Amnesia                   Affiliation : Amnesia Leader       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What is your current postion in the group Amnesia?                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  LES : I'm in a leader of Amnesia.                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : How did Amnesia came about?                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  LES : Amnesia came about when a few of us decided to leave the courier    บ
 บ        group MALiCE, because of personal and miscellaneous conflicts       บ
 บ        along with some other problems.  We decided to start our own        บ
 บ        group.  The name was just thrown in there.                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : When Amnesia started, did you guys face any serious problems?       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  LES : We ran into a few problems, one was with Captain Blood.  He was     บ
 บ        one of the few people that we started the group with originally.    บ
 บ        He caused a lot of problems and split off to form his own group.    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Is Captian Blood's group still messing with Amnesia, or his group   บ
 บ        pretty much dead?                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  LES : Captain Blood's group is still alive, but he was kicked out of it.  บ
 บ        They are cool with us and don't fuck with us anymore.               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What was the name of the Captain Blood's courier group?             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  LES : The name was, and still is Rapier.                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : I noticed that Amnesia and Digital held a friendly competition,     บ
 บ        what was that all about?                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  LES : It was suggested by a courier in Amnesia to compete against         บ
 บ        Digital.  Eventually, I agreed to it and 6 Amnesia couriers         บ
 บ        competed with 15 Digital couriers on a site for a week.  The        บ
 บ        competition ended on May 2, 1996, about an hour ago.                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What was the result of the competition?                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  LES : Amnesia won by about 30 megs or so.  It was fairly close toward     บ
 บ        the end, but there was alot of crap uploaded by both sides, so it   บ
 บ        wasn't really that fun.                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Is Amnesia better in Internet couriering or BBS couriering?         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  LES : Amnesia is equally good in both aspects of couriering.              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What does one have to do to become an Amnesia member?               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  LES : The Internet division is closed, but the BBS division requires      บ
 บ        that you trade long distance and that you do about 200 megs a       บ
 บ        week.                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Is Amnesia "official couriers" for any release groups?              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  LES : We have a few "unofficial" officials, but I have not agreed to      บ
 บ        officially courier for any release group as of yet.                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Is the summer of 1996 going to have a major impact on Amnesia?      บ
 บ        Most SiteOps are in college and take leave during the summer, and   บ
 บ        as result, many FTP sites go down.                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  LES : I don't think it will have a big effect on Amnesia.                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : How old is Amnesia, and what are Amnesia's future plans?            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  LES : We have been around for 2 months now.  Our future plans are to      บ
 บ        just to have more fun by moving some files, etc.                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What makes Amnesia different from any other group?                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  LES : We just try to have fun and we try not get too involved in the      บ
 บ        politics of it all, at least I try not to.                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What is your general feeling toward the scene?                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  LES : I feel that the scene is going down the tubes.  There is too much   บ
 บ        back stabbing and ego trips.  It's gotten way out of hand.  It's    บ
 บ        supposed to be a fun hobby, an escape from reality,people take it   บ
 บ        way too seriously though.  They ought to just lighten up and have   บ
 บ        some fun.                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Reporter : Super Hacker              Interviewee : Silent Mobius        บ
 บ    Subject  : Digital                   Affiliation : Digital Leader       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What is your current position in Digital?                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SMO : I am the founder and one of the leaders.                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : When did Digital come into being?                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SMO : I'd have to say last year, probably around September.               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : As Digital came into being did it had any problem or conflicts      บ
 บ        with other groups?                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SMO : No, at least I don't think so.  I always avoided trouble.  We       บ
 บ        might have had some trouble with MindCrash.                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Can you give us some background information on Digital?             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SMO : Devast and I both used to be in MindCrash, when The Wicked One and  บ
 บ        Avoozl ran it.  When I first joined, I didn't know much political   บ
 บ        things about it.  All I knew is that it was a plain old couriering  บ
 บ        group, and I became a senior, then what happened was, I found out   บ
 บ        that The Wicked One didn't like Devast too much.  Devast said that  บ
 บ        he would courier whenever he wanted to.  He'd courier nothing and   บ
 บ        then sometimes he does 150 megs.  The Wicked One said that he was   บ
 บ        going to kick Devast out of MindCrash but Devast decided to quit    บ
 บ        before he'd get kicked out.  So be it, and I found out about it,    บ
 บ        but didn't care at first.  Then The Wicked One and Avoozl got a     บ
 บ        job together, and were busy; I tried to take care of MindCrash,     บ
 บ        but none of the couriers respected me like a senior.  I got pissed  บ
 บ        and left.  Then I met Devast, and he decided to start a couriering  บ
 บ        group with me.  At first, it was going to be Devast, Creed,         บ
 บ        Desolation Angel and me, but then Desolation Angel dropped out.     บ
 บ        Devast and I were debating on a name, and came up with Digital and  บ
 บ        that's how it all started...                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Which other courier groups are currently competing with Digital?    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SMO : We're not really in competition; we were just challenged into a     บ
 บ        competition with Amnesia, and Devast decided to go for it, but I    บ
 บ        wouldn't call it an actual competition.                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Will you call this a friendly competition, or something that just   บ
 บ        keeps the group on their toes?                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SMO : I'd consider it kind of both.  We have a great bunch of guys in     บ
 บ        Digital; no egos, nothing.  We're out just to have fun and to       บ
 บ        courier, but I wouldn't call it a rivalry between the two groups.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Is the summer of 1996 going to have a major impact on Digital?      บ
 บ        Most SiteOps are in college and take leave during the summer, and   บ
 บ        as result, many FTP sites go down.                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SMO : Not too sure, I dont' really know.  Actually it all depends on the  บ
 บ        couriers and SiteOps themselves.  I mean, we are a serious group,   บ
 บ        but at same time, a lot of us have fun at it...                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : So Digital is not worried about the summer time blues?  Because     บ
 บ        summer is when several groups come up and many go out because like  บ
 บ        I said several group members go out of town and sites go down.      บ
 บ        Digital is not worried about that all?                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SMO : Well, we are worried, but eventually, summer will end, so things    บ
 บ        will go back to normal I guess, but it's all so unpredictable.      บ
 บ        There's nothing I can do about it even if I'm worried.              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : How does the competition between Amnesia and Digital work?          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SMO : You see, we upload to see who gets more within the week.  I'm not   บ
 บ        really into it.  Devast organized it and all on BBX, and it's       บ
 บ        going out pretty fun.  I don't really care who wins or loses        บ
 บ        actually, the whole point is just to upload.                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Do you have any last few comments towards the scene?                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SMO : For one thing, I am starting to see what Cyber Angel meant when he  บ
 บ        said "It's pointless to move other peoples' files."  Releasing      บ
 บ        groups are the big time winners easily.  But towards Digital,       บ
 บ        well, we've made quite a bit of improvement with some merges, and   บ
 บ        we don't have no egos flying, so it's going out pretty good, and    บ
 บ        we're keeping the competition between Amnesia really tight, even    บ
 บ        though they have a couple of great couriers.                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Uploading other peoples file is hard work.  There's only a certain  บ
 บ        amount of uploading each group can do.  No group can call every     บ
 บ        BBS in the world to upload all their new releases, and Digital as   บ
 บ        a group is putting alot of effort moving the warez, and that is     บ
 บ        suffice to say that courier groups are needed in order for the      บ
 บ        scene to thrive.                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SMO : Thanks, we're just doing our share for the scene.  As for calling   บ
 บ        every BBS, it's just the speed of it that you get it on.  And       บ
 บ        believe me, it is hard work.                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Is Digital better in Internet couriering or BBS couriering?         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SMO : Digital is better off in Internet courieriering.  Several of our    บ
 บ        BBS coordinators left the scene or have lost their Internet         บ
 บ        accounts (What a coincidence...), but now, we are going to rebuild  บ
 บ        the BBS division once more.                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 บ    Reporter : Hitex                     Interviewee : Everclear            บ
 บ    Subject  : RiSC/RZR/SCUM             Affiliation : RiSC/RZR/SCUM        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : You've 3 main affiliations, RiSC (Rise in Superior Couriering),     บ
 บ        Razor 1911, and Scum.  What made you choose those groups?           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  EVR : Well, RiSC and Razor 1911 are the best, and I'm friends with Third  บ
 บ        Son so I decided to joined Scum.                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What is your position in each one of the groups?                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  EVR : I'm a bulletin board courier in all three.                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What do you think puts RiSC on top and has kept it there for so     บ
 บ        long?                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  EVR : RiSC has the finest traders, bulletin boards, and FTP sites         บ
 บ        around.  We dominate both the Internet and the boards.  Everyone    บ
 บ        works their assess off, and we have quality leaders.                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Razor 1911 has also been around for a long time, but lately it has  บ
 บ        been getting a lot of competition from such groups as Dynamix,      บ
 บ        Hybrid, and Napalm.  Do you think that Razor 1911 is still #1 in    บ
 บ        the games scene?                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  EVR : Yes, of course.  Not to group bash, but we release quality,         บ
 บ        WORKING releases.  The best games are always released by Razor      บ
 บ        1911.  We also have the best trading team of any games group.       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Well I don't doubt that it worked, but a couple of days ago Razor   บ
 บ        1911 released Tyrian.  Was that a real release?                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  EVR : Yes, that was newer version of Tyrian.  If people would have        บ
 บ        looked closely they would have noticed that, it wasn't a dupe.      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Yeah, I didn't think it was because it didn't get nuked anywhere.   บ
 บ        Well, that's cool, in that case, I'll go download it, I heard it's  บ
 บ        an awesome game.  What do you think of Napalm?  I've seen them      บ
 บ        beat out Razor 1911 in release numbers, what do you think this      บ
 บ        means?                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  EVR : I think that while Razor 1911 is busy making their releases WORK,   บ
 บ        Napalm is releasing the game, then releasing a crack 10 days        บ
 บ        later.  From now on, Razor 1911 will still release a game even if   บ
 บ        Napalm has already released it.                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : That sounds like a plan.  What do you think about RiSC's policy to  บ
 บ        support only "top 10" boards?                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  EVR : I think it makes sense.  Why bother with other boards?  They're     บ
 บ        too easy!  RiSC members need to go where the competition is :)      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Don't you think that the small multinode boards deserve some        บ
 บ        support, though?                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  EVR : If they are RiSC, then I am sure they get support, but more effort  บ
 บ        goes into the bigger boards, RiSC is more net based then BBS based  บ
 บ        anyhow.                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Are you referring to IRC on the Internet or FTP sites?              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  EVR : FTP sites, RiSC is #1 on every site, guaranteed.                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What are the requirements to become a courier for RiSC?             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  EVR : There are no set requirements, anyone that can do the job can get   บ
 บ        in.  RiSC is the hardest courier group to get into though.          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : How many hours per week do you spend couriering for RiSC?  What is  บ
 บ        the job description of being a RiSC member?                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  EVR : I'll tell you this, I spend a LOT of time couriering.  It's a lot   บ
 บ        of work.                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : About Scum, what is your feeling towards the general consensus      บ
 บ        that Scum came back only to reiterate its past glories and that it  บ
 บ        is failing pathetically compared to its old potential as one of     บ
 บ        the scene's leading utils groups?                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  EVR : If that's what people think, well, Scum will get better, it's       บ
 บ        really just based on a bunch of friends hanging out.  If we aren't  บ
 บ        the #1 in utils, no big deal.                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : That's an awesome attitude, it is only through calmness and trust   บ
 บ        in time that a group gets better.  What do you have to say to the   บ
 บ        wealth that left Scum for PWA (Pirates with Attitudes)?             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  EVR : Well, PWA is #1 right now, so it makes sense that good suppliers    บ
 บ        go with the best utils group.                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ    Reporter : Super Hacker              Interviewee : Rapid Motion         บ
 บ    Subject  : Hostile                   Affiliation : Hostile Leader       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What is your current position in Hostile?                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RAP : I am the founder and leader of Hostile.                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : How old is Hostile, and what type of group is it?                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RAP : Hostile was formed in late January early February of 96.  We        บ
 บ        currently release utils and PPEs (PCBoard Programming Executable).  บ
 บ        We used to release both games and utils, but we no longer release   บ
 บ        both.                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Why don't you release both games and utils anymore?                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RAP : We used to release both games and utils but we have narrowed it     บ
 บ        down to just utils and PPEs because we have a sister group called   บ
 บ        Lensmen which is our games division.  We give Lensmen our games     บ
 บ        and in turn, they give us their utils.                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : When Hositle was first created, did it come upon any problems such  บ
 บ        as splits or break ups?                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RAP : Not at first, but then we started coming upon an onslaught of       บ
 บ        problems when I made Perfect Form a leader in Hostile.  He took     บ
 บ        advantage of the position I gave him and he tried to split up my    บ
 บ        group.  I then kicked him and that drove Hostile into a low point   บ
 บ        in the scene.  After kicking him from the group, there were some    บ
 บ        members that were uncertain what direction the group was taking.    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : When you kicked Perfect Form out of Hostile, did it backfire?  Did  บ
 บ        your group suffer significantly?  Most group members like to        บ
 บ        follow their leader, and since you and Perfect Form were leader,    บ
 บ        did they have a hard time picking between who to follow?            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RAP : No, Perfect Form was a leader ranked below me.  I had a few         บ
 บ        members that followed me.  Most of the great members stuck with     บ
 บ        Hostile and did not follow Perfect Form because he was doing some   บ
 บ        very lame things. In the end, Perfect Form's expulsion              บ
 บ        strengthened Hostile and we got BETTER suppliers.  All my old       บ
 บ        active suppliers came back to the group, and the group is still     บ
 บ        under construction somewhat but it is now doing better and is       บ
 บ        stronger than it has been.                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What are your future plans for Hostile?                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RAP : I will like to strengthen the group more and get Hostile more       บ
 บ        noticed in the utils scene.  I am strenghtening Hostile by making   บ
 บ        it a more stable group, and to do that, we're working on brining    บ
 บ        more quality releases to the scene.                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : How does one become a member of Hostile?  Are there any positions   บ
 บ        available in Hostile?                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RAP : Hostile has an application WHQ (Tower of Sorcery) that is still     บ
 บ        under construction.  We also have special application PPEs on       บ
 บ        Shroom's board, and we also offer our applications on IRC.          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Is Hostile in the scene to become #1 by ruining the competition or  บ
 บ        is it just here for fun?                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RAP : We have places in the group for those who are productive            บ
 บ        suppliers.  We also have room for FAST traders and for those who    บ
 บ        wish to code PPEs, etc.  Anyone who has something to offer is       บ
 บ        welcome to the group.  We are here for personal satisfaction, and   บ
 บ        that's what it's all about.                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : So bascially, Hostile is not here for the competition and is not    บ
 บ        actively looking for competition?  Is my assumption correct?        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RAP : In a sense, yes, we would like to compete but we're not planning    บ
 บ        to lose any sleep if we cannot compete with DOD or PWA.             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : When Hostile does start to compete, which other utils groups will   บ
 บ        be it's major competiton?                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RAP : Hostile is currently competing with COPS, Pinnacle, Scum, and       บ
 บ        X-Force.  I don't think we are ready to compete with DOD or PWA     บ
 บ        yet.  Hostile is here to stay, and we hope to gain the same         บ
 บ        respect we give to other groups.                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 บ    Reporter : Rebel Chicken             Interviewee : Perfect Form         บ
 บ    Subject  : Perfect Form              Affiliation : Ex-Hostile Leader    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : A few months ago, you were kicked out of Demolition despite the     บ
 บ        fact that you were a senior in that group.  You were accused of     บ
 บ        stealing suppliers for a rival group.  However, that accusation     บ
 บ        was proved to be false since you were not trying to steal           บ
 บ        suppliers, but you were trying to steal artists.  But that is       บ
 บ        ancient history.  In the recent weeks, you were again kicked out    บ
 บ        of a group you were supposedly a "leader/senior" of.  You were      บ
 บ        kicked out of Hostile because you were again attempting to steal    บ
 บ        members, breaking up the group, and causing havoc.  What do you     บ
 บ        have to say about your recent "kicked in the ass by your own        บ
 บ        group?"                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  PER : Well, I was in Hostile.                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : I know that.                                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  PER : I did everyting for that group and I put in 100% effort.  It was a  บ
 บ        good group when I was in it, when I was running the show.           บ
 บ        However, Rapid Motion knows DICK SHIT.  I have not tried to break   บ
 บ        up the group in any way whatsoever.  Rapid Motion is making up      บ
 บ        bullshit again.                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : You admit that you gave 100% for the group, what exactly did you    บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : So you played such a major role in Hostile, that when you left, it  บ
 บ        could not survive without you?  ONE person killed the group?        บ
 บ        *YOU* basically killed the WHOLE group, and you didn't even take    บ
 บ        anyone with you?  I could believe if 75% of the group left          บ
 บ        Hostile, and then it culdn't function, but how could 1 person       บ
 บ        leaving devastate the group so much?                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  PER : I put in 100% effort to making sure that Hostile would survive      บ
 บ        when I was in it.  Why did it die?  Well, because I had brought     บ
 บ        everyone in it and I knew how to run a group and it released        บ
 บ        almost everyday and every member worked their asses off.  When I    บ
 บ        left, nearly all the suppliers and couriers left for other groups.  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : The fact that you brought in a lot of members that didn't do        บ
 บ        anything for the group is what caused so much trouble for Hostile.  บ
 บ        You brought in too many lamers who didn't know what they were       บ
 บ        doing or did nothing, and the suppliers that you did help bring     บ
 บ        into the group only supplied dupes, and that in your 100% effort    บ
 บ        to make it a good group, you essentially killed it.  Then I must    บ
 บ        ask, what group you did join after you left Hostile, and where did  บ
 บ        "nearly all the suppliers and couriers" leave for (which other      บ
 บ        group)?  Why did they join other groups?  Why did not follow you    บ
 บ        around since you were their true leader?  Or perhaps, you           บ
 บ        overrated your own leadership and importance, and the rest of       บ
 บ        Hostile saw that, and that can be why they did not follow you       บ
 บ        either.                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  PER : Yes, I have to admit I brought in a couple of lamers, and           บ
 บ        suppliers that supplied dupes, but most of the supplies did supply  บ
 บ        unreleased utils.  I have no idea where "nearly all the suppliers   บ
 บ        and couriers" went to after Hostile split up.                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Okay, now that we have it clear that *YOU* ran Hostile, then what   บ
 บ        did the Rapid Motion (the other leader) do?  Did he just sit on     บ
 บ        his ass watching you give 100% for HIS group?  What's the deal      บ
 บ        with him?                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  PER : Rapid Motion just sat there watching me do everything, proclaiming  บ
 บ        himself leader when he did nothing.  All he would do is, logon and  บ
 บ        see how everything was going, and then he'd log right back off.     บ
 บ        ALL I have to say is, ask anyone what Hostile was like when I was   บ
 บ        running it.  Ever since i left, it's become a crappy utils group.   บ

 บ  PER : I did.                                                              บ
