 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Lucifers Fear                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Charges Laid                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  The following articles are based on information obtained from "The        บ
 บ  Chronicle-Journal" Saturday, April 20, 1996.                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A city man, known as "The Anarchist" on IRC, will be appearing in     บ
 บ  the Ontario Court's provincial division May 7 facing nine charges         บ
 บ  relating to child pornography and pirated software.                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Geza Tibor Arnoth, 18, of 417 Brown St. faces seven Criminal Code     บ
 บ  and two copywright charges in connection with the operation of a          บ
 บ  computer bulletin board which was seized in January.  Police allege that  บ
 บ  Arnoth was running an electronic bulletin board that offered child        บ
 บ  pornography and pirated software to anyone who had a mdoem and computer   บ
 บ  to download the material.                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A modem is a device that turns data from your computer into a signal  บ
 บ  that can be transmitted over a telephone line.  The computer at the       บ
 บ  other end of the telephone connection also requires a modem.              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Arnoth was charged with the following offenses :                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                * Possession of obscene material for the purpose of         บ
 บ                  distribution.                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                * Distribution of obscene material.                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                * Possession of crime comics for the purpose of             บ
 บ                  distribution.                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                * Distribution of crime comics.                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                * Possession of child pornography.                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                * Possession of child pornography for the purpose of        บ
 บ                  distribution.                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                * Distribution of child pornography.                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                * Offering, by way of trade, copywright protected           บ
 บ                  software.                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                * Distribution of copyright protected software.             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      RCMP Const. Tom James and Thunder Bay Police Det. Brian Peltonen had  บ
 บ  been sifting through thousands of graphic and text files over the past    บ
 บ  three months since they seized two computers in Westfort on Jan. 23.      บ
 บ  Although this was the first case in Thunder Bay, police say child         บ
 บ  pornography via the Internet and electronic bulletin boards are the most  บ
 บ  common forms of distribtution.  James said earlier some of the messages   บ
 บ  they had found on the bulletin board "scary but not surprising."  Police  บ
 บ  had been gathering evidence since January and chose to execute search     บ
 บ  warrants over a few days in March to try to surprise people operating     บ
 บ  bulletin boards.  James said if suspects knew ahead of time they would    บ
 บ  be investigated, they could just pull the plug, delete files or copy      บ
 บ  them onto disks and hide them.                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Cyberspace is like a lot of other places.  Go looking for trouble     บ
 บ  and you're likely find it.  When it comes to the Internet, there are      บ
 บ  resources for people who would deny the Holocaust, for those looking for  บ
 บ  detailed instructions on making pipe bombs, and, as Thunder Bay recently  บ
 บ  learned, for those interested in the distribution of child pornography.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Thunder Bay RCMP charged 18-year-old Geza Tibor Arnoth Friday with    บ
 บ  seven criminal charges.  Arnoth is charged with running an electronic     บ
 บ  bulletin board accessible via the Internet that offered child             บ
 บ  pornography and pirated software to anyone who had a modem and computer   บ
 บ  to download the material.                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      At present there's little to prevent people in Northwestern Ontario   บ
 บ  from acquiring child pornography - if they are determined enough to       บ
 บ  search for it on the Internet.  That's because the material Arnoth is     บ
 บ  charged with distributing is just like a drop in a very large bucket.     บ
 บ  Using widely-available Internet search tools such as Alta Vista and       บ
 บ  Yahoo, anyone with an Internet account can find dozens of Internet        บ
 บ  newsgroups, web pages and other electronic resources catering to child    บ
 บ  pornographers and pedophilla.  Some of those recources are nothing more   บ
 บ  than a lot of dirty words; other recources enable an Internet surfer to   บ
 บ  access graphic decipitions of sexual acts involving minors.               บ
 บ  Representitaves of the North American Man/Boy Love Association, for       บ
 บ  instance, show up in newsgroups arguing in favour of consensual sex       บ
 บ  between adults and 10-year-old boys.  While he topic of their discussion  บ
 บ  may not be for everyone, the language they use seems to be no worse than  บ
 บ  that found in a newspaper editorial.  It's difficult to gauge the extent  บ
 บ  of pornography on the Internet.  It's even more difficult in many cases   บ
 บ  for police to track down the perpetrators.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A Thunder Bay resident, for instance, could distribute pornography    บ
 บ  from a computer located in the Philippines.  While police try to sort     บ
 บ  out international jurisdictional and legal issues, a pornographer could   บ
 บ  be switching the computer distribution point to Poland or any number of   บ
 บ  countries.                                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Cracking Internet pornography rings requires police with              บ
 บ  sophisticated new tools.  It also requires applying what are in many      บ
 บ  cases arcane laws to very modern circumstances.  Internet groups          บ
 บ  estimate there may be as many as 20 to 60 million Internet users around   บ
 บ  the world, the vast majority of whom, as Internet advocates will say,     บ
 บ  use the global network of computers for largely legtimate purposes.       บ
 บ  Still, one Finnish researcher tried to get a handle on child pornography  บ
 บ  in a survey last year.                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Researcher Mats Wiklund monitored four Internet newsgroups that deal  บ
 บ  with pornographic pictures for one week in late 1995.  Newsgroups are     บ
 บ  part of the Internet in which users can exchange electronic messages.     บ
 บ  Among the images he saw were eight pictures of children Wiklund           บ
 บ  estimated to be between eight and 13 years old.  He reported that none    บ
 บ  of the pictures show intercourse or other explicit sexual activity,       บ
 บ  although five of the pictures had text on them offering more pictures of  บ
 บ  nude children through electronic bulletin boards and electronic mail.     บ
 บ  But as many Internet authorities have pointed out since then, it's        บ
 บ  difficult to take Wiklund's survey as representative because the quality  บ
 บ  and quantity of Internet information can change radically from day to     บ
 บ  day.                                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Despite the difficulty of tracking down pornographers, many           บ
 บ  governments are trying to pass new laws to make Internet distribution of  บ
 บ  pornography illegal.  The U.S. recently passed the controversial          บ
 บ  Communications Decency Act which its critics say is too broad and         บ
 บ  restricts free speech.  The Canadian government has not yet passed any    บ
 บ  such laws, although it is under pressure to do so.                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      At this point, then, it is up to individual Internet users to act as  บ
 บ  their own censor.  Parents of Internet users can purchase software        บ
 บ  products that prevent access to certain parts of the Internet.  Beyond    บ
 บ  that, groups of Internet users can petition their Internet provider to    บ
 บ  make certain Internet services unavailable.  Still, because much          บ
 บ  sexually explicit material is available through private electronic        บ
 บ  bullents boards, such as the one Arnoth is accused of operating,          บ
 บ  pornography is still going to be there for those determined to get it.    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ฐ ฐฐ ฐ ฿฿ฐ ฐ฿ ฿฿ ฐ  ฿฿฿฿฿฿฿ ฐ  ฿ฐฐฐฐฐฐ ฐฐฐ
        ฿        ฐ฿฿฿฿฿฿   ฿฿       ฿฿

 บ    Author  : Lucifers Fear                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Tom James Makes His Visit                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      In the last few months, Tom James who is known as a famous local      บ
 บ  RCMP officer in Thunder Bay, Ontario, Canada who busted "The Shadow       บ
 บ  Lands" which was ran by The Anarchist who was a member of Demolition and  บ
 บ  Legacy, recently visited local high schools to give warnings around.  He  บ
 บ  made a stop at almost every school to do a 2 hour presentation on         บ
 บ  piracy, pornography and hacking.                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The main articles that were pointed out during his boring             บ
 บ  presentation were stories on pornography, stories on hacking, and of      บ
 บ  course, stories on piracy.  Being so lucky, he picked me as the one to    บ
 บ  answer every law and punishment concerning piracy. Answering his          บ
 บ  questions, possession and distribution of piracy in Canada could result   บ
 บ  with a 10 years or up to life in prison, and/or fines up to a million     บ
 บ  dollars along with a civil suit.                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      After his presentation, I had a talk with him myself.  He informed    บ
 บ  me that I was still under investigation and liable for prosecution        บ
 บ  because The Anarchist has pointed his finger at me for all the blame.     บ
 บ  What a fucker, he has no evidence on me.                 I questioned     บ
 บ  him about the procedure of busting bulletin boards in Canada, he said     บ
 บ  you have to get on, be able to download warez without vilolating any      บ
 บ  crimes, then put the file(s) on diskette and test them out.  Also, since  บ
 บ  I was bored I asked him on the use of disclaimers on bulletin boards      บ
 บ  since they are used so often on many U.S. bulletin boards.  He laughed    บ
 บ  and said to me, "So what, I'm a cop.  Does that mean I can't get on a     บ
 บ  bulletin board?"  Obviously he has no clue about anything because that    บ
 บ  would mean he is violating his own ass, considering that the dumbass      บ
 บ  goes on local bulletin boards asking questions on oneliners such as       บ
 บ  "Anyone know where I can get some cool pirated software?  I'm bored."     บ
 บ  Furthermore, this goes to show that Tom James is another example of the   บ
 บ  one we all love, Chris Carter.  So if you want to speak with this damn    บ
 บ  crawfish shrimp-smellin' cunt dirty whore cunt fucking biatch!, call his  บ
 บ  office at (807) 623-2791 and ask for Tom James.                           บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Frost                                                         บ
 บ    Subject : Amnesia vs. Digital                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Between the dates of 04/26/96 and 05/03/96, two trading groups,       บ
 บ  Amnesia and Digital, set out to compete in an upload contest.  This       บ
 บ  competition was the result of some childish bickering over which group    บ
 บ  was better.  This ultimately ended in a competition, which, after all,    บ
 บ  is what courier groups are for!  The guidelines for the competition were  บ
 บ  that Amnesia be allowed 6 traders and Digital 15.  For the record,        บ
 บ  Digital did not require all 15, but Amnesia insisted we take 15 traders.  บ
 บ  The site to which we were to compete on was BBX.                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      To give you a little background information on who is who, I will     บ
 บ  talk about my opinions as a Digital trader.  Digital is a courier group   บ
 บ  that was formed by Devast and Silent Mobius.  Digital is, in my opinion,  บ
 บ  one of the better couriering groups in the scene today.  It is limited    บ
 บ  only by its organization and resources.  Although our organization is     บ
 บ  very good, we lack the ability to cater to the widely diverse traders.    บ
 บ  Our group does not depend on a single dictator or council, but            บ
 บ  individuals that make decisions for themselves.  Digital has a            บ
 บ  thoroughly different style of couriering when it comes to competition.    บ
 บ  I think our competing style is many times better, but at the same time    บ
 บ  our board and other sections are completely neglected.  I think this is   บ
 บ  a pretty good assessment of Digital.  Our only major problem is a lack    บ
 บ  of traders on the top sites.                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      As for my opinion of Amnesia, as a group, I think they are one of     บ
 บ  the best at doing what they do.  I really know very little about their    บ
 บ  group as a whole and how they run their ship, so I won't comment there.   บ
 บ  Suffice it to say that this group shows much promise.                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Now that you've heard about the groups, let's talk about the          บ
 บ  competition.  This competition was not what I would have expected.        บ
 บ  There were many severe problems that confused both groups in this         บ
 บ  ordeal.                                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      First off, the decision of the site to which we were to courier to    บ
 บ  lead to many problems.  BBX is a fast site in terms of new warez, but     บ
 บ  when all the Digital and Amnesia couriers raced to BBX, there weren't     บ
 บ  enough user slots to support them.  When the SiteOp graciously added      บ
 บ  more slots, the speed of transfers and the overall performance of the     บ
 บ  board dropped.  In his words it was a lose/lose situation.  The more      บ
 บ  slots he added, the poorer the performance.  Many release disks were      บ
 บ  lost on Digital's side, and I'd imagine the same was true for Amnesia.    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Secondly, the Amnesia traders had nuke access on BBX, and there was   บ
 บ  foul play to say the least.  I will not dwell on the topic because I      บ
 บ  would not want to embarass anyone.  Also, many of my resources were       บ
 บ  sabotaged during and before the competition.  I allowed Pericles to use   บ
 บ  my account and therefore gain access to his sites.  There was much        บ
 บ  debate, and in the end, I must say that I should have respected the       บ
 บ  SiteOp's rules, and am sorry for using their sites without permision.     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Many people say that I was using the accounts unjustly and I was not  บ
 บ  a good trader without those sites.  I must concur, because any trader     บ
 บ  without his resourecs is nothing, you can only be as fast as your         บ
 บ  resources allow you to be.  I feel bad for losing the sites, but not as   บ
 บ  bad as I feel for those of you that got them taken away from me.          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Thirdly, and worst of all, there was intense competition and group    บ
 บ  pride.  Name calling and bickering were rampant.  There was a bit of      บ
 บ  bitterness in the whole area, brought upon by big egos clashing.  I am    บ
 บ  sorry for any bickering I may have participated in, in general, I'm sure  บ
 บ  we all look at the arguments as petty and childish.                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I think it is safe to say both groups are severely competitive when   บ
 บ  threatened.  This competition was started when Digital felt that it was   บ
 บ  being discredited by Amnesia.  When an Amnesia courier stepped over the   บ
 บ  line, it was all a chain reaction from there, egos and group pride led    บ
 บ  to a competition. It is my opinion that this competition has brought out  บ
 บ  the worst in both groups.  I'm sure all our egos got the bet of us at     บ
 บ  one point.  However, it is all necessary to prove our "worth."            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The final score of the competition was 702 Digital and 729 Amnesia.   บ
 บ  This was based on a week-long competition held at BBX; Amnesia's U.S.     บ
 บ  Headquarters (nice site BTW).  15 Digital traders and 6 Amnesia traders   บ
 บ  went at it (Although I think no more than 7 Digital traders actually      บ
 บ  uploaded).  It was a battle to say the least.  I must say Dark Eclipse    บ
 บ  from Digital stole the show by uploading 347 or so megs holding the top   บ
 บ  uploader out of both groups.                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      At the very beginning of the competition, I think Digital started     บ
 บ  strong, however after a nuke on a massive release, Digital fell behind.   บ
 บ  By the end of day 1, Digital reaffirmed its grasp with a small lead.      บ
 บ  Digital led for the majority of the contest until Wednesday where in one  บ
 บ  leap, Amnesia managed to upload some 250 megs taking the leady by         บ
 บ  approximtely 200 megs.  On Thursday (the last day) Digital began          บ
 บ  uploading massively and began narrowing down the margin.  Then we got     บ
 บ  news that a release that Amnesia had uploaded was nuked (100 megs).       บ
 บ  With a massive 55 disk release in hand, Digital was ready to take first   บ
 บ  place, however complications with BBX's user limit and idling traders     บ
 บ  made it impossible to do so.                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Many people helped Digital along the way, and I'd like to take the    บ
 บ  time to thank them.  RiSC, thanks for all the support!  fATE, thanks for  บ
 บ  the emotional support!                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      According to Trite, RiSC is #1, MALiCe is #2, Amnesia is #3, Digital  บ
 บ  is #4, and Everlast is #5.  I don't think he is in the position to        บ
 บ  judge, however, because he knows so little about both Digital and         บ
 บ  Amnesia.  Some of the information in his "Review" was completely false,   บ
 บ  and I do believe that Amnesia has the #2 position to say the least.       บ
 บ  MALiCE is good, but Amnesia is sporting some of the best Internet         บ
 บ  traders in the scene (Prozac, Davan, etc.).  I think all groups have      บ
 บ  their ups and downs, so we shall see.                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Super Hacker                                                  บ
 บ    Subject : Revenge on Piracy                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  The following article is based on information obtained from newspapers    บ
 บ  and magazines.                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The Business Software Alliance estimates that software piracy steals  บ
 บ  more than $15 billion a year from the coffers of software publishers and  บ
 บ  it is for that reason that Congress is preparing to shore up the laws     บ
 บ  dealing with using the Internet for piracy purposes.                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      In early November 1995 the first hearings were held before a joint    บ
 บ  session of the Senate Judiciary Committee and the House Judiciary         บ
 บ  Subcommittee to begin taking testimony on the new NII Copyright           บ
 บ  Protection Act (H.R.2441 and S. 1284).  The National Information          บ
 บ  Infrastructure or NII is what the Internet is referred to by the          บ
 บ  government.  The Copyright Protection Act is designed to ensure that      บ
 บ  copyrighted works are fully protected on the Internet and other           บ
 บ  telecommunications networks.                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      This move to shore-up the copyright laws comes on the heels of some   บ
 บ  high-profile criminal cases.  Thomas Nick Alefantes of Los Angeles was    บ
 บ  arrested in November after the L.A district Attorney's Office and         บ
 บ  antipiracy investigators raided his home following allegations that he    บ
 บ  operated a software piracy operation.  Lawmen seized $1 million worth of  บ
 บ  illegally copied software.  Alefantes, known on-line as Captain Blood,    บ
 บ  sold and rented pirated software after advertising in trade magazines.    บ
 บ  Autodesk Inc, CEO Carl Bartz was quoted in Wall Street Journal as saying  บ
 บ  she was grateful for Alefantes's arrest because, "...our losses over the  บ
 บ  past five years from this man's alleged activities add to millions of     บ
 บ  dollars..."                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Alefantes was charged with two felony counts of fraud and trademark   บ
 บ  violations with bail set at a quarter million dollars.  All this          บ
 บ  attention to the pirating of very expensive productivity programs will    บ
 บ  surely cast a spotlight on the widespread pirating of computer games.     บ
 บ  Most of this pirating is more like two, three, or four friends buying     บ
 บ  one copy of a game and then copying it for distribution among             บ
 บ  themselves.  But even this has software publishers up in arms.  Software  บ
 บ  developers AND publishers are seriously concerned about the unauthorized  บ
 บ  copying and trafficking of software.  The Internet's future as a          บ
 บ  commercial distribution channel is big, says Jay Willbur of Id Software.  บ
 บ  "My company's software is routinely pirated on the Internet, even before  บ
 บ  it's released."                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Wilbur was joined in supporting the Copyright Protection Act by the   บ
 บ  Software Publishers Association.  SPA counsel Mark Traphagen says the     บ
 บ  new act is targeted toward criminal intentions, but what about teenagers  บ
 บ  who feel pirating games like copying their favorite music CD, is okay?    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      "In general" Traphagen says, "the legislation will not change the     บ
 บ  attitudes of those children who think that copyright infringement is      บ
 บ  okay.   What will change those attitudes is education and both the SPA    บ
 บ  and the U.S. government have made a commitment in educating the next      บ
 บ  generation of computer software users about how important it is to        บ
 บ  respect copyrights, both on and off the Internet."                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      For nearly a year, the SPA and other concerned groups and companies   บ
 บ  have pooled their resources to convince software users not to pirate      บ
 บ  software.  Part of this effort is the "Don't Copy That Floppy Campaign".  บ
 บ  Traphagen says there are no plans to hunt down teen pirates, but this     บ
 บ  act is the beginning of legislation that will ensure that there are       บ
 บ  safeguards in place in order that they can do business on the Internet    บ
 บ  without losing their financial shirts because of piracy.                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      "It's going to help promote the commercial development of some parts  บ
 บ  of the Internet," he says, "In several ways.  First of all it's going to  บ
 บ  clarify what we believe is existing law, which is the transmissions of    บ
 บ  copyrighted works, including software, are fully protected by copyright   บ
 บ  law."                                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Traphagen says the act would remove any doubt that software           บ
 บ  copyright infringements can and will be dealt with as in the Alefantes    บ
 บ  case.  One of the new provisions of the act would prohibit the            บ
 บ  manufacture, sale or use of so called "Black boxes," which are devices    บ
 บ  or services, including software theater used to circumvent encryption or  บ
 บ  copy protection.  Taphagen says this is already part of the law dealing   บ
 บ  with encrypted satellite television broadcasts and the SPA wants to see   บ
 บ  this extended to the Internet and on-line transmissions as well.          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      As the supporting lobbying groups begin to voice their wants the act  บ
 บ  could include more provisions such as making copyright infringements a    บ
 บ  crime even if there is no private financial gain.  That strikes very      บ
 บ  close to home for gamers.  More testimony is expected in the first        บ
 บ  quarter of 1996 before both committees and the new NII Copyright          บ
 บ  Protections Act is expected to become law late in 1996.                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Krypto                                                        บ
 บ    Subject : "passwd"                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      At times many of us are without Internet shell account, therefore     บ
 บ  inhibiting our ablility to spread warez.  Many of us seek to remedy the   บ
 บ  situation by cracking a few Internet shell accounts, and then using them  บ
 บ  to suit our needs.  The following are a few techniques expert crackers    บ
 บ  use when they are in the process of cracking UNIX accounts.               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Most Internet shells are UNIX based and therefore store the password  บ
 บ  of all their users in a file called "passwd".  This is usually located    บ
 บ  at the path /etc/passwd.  The "passwd" file contains lines looking like   บ
 บ  this :                                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  bgates:VKa0XuF8KB4sc:5604:12:William Gates:/home/bgates:/bin/bash         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Essentially, the line is broken down into these parts :               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Username: bgates                                                          บ
 บ  Encrypted Password: VKa0XuF8KB4sc                                         บ
 บ  User number: 5604                                                         บ
 บ  Group Number: 12                                                          บ
 บ  Real Name (usually): William Gates                                        บ
 บ  Home Directory: /home/bgates                                              บ
 บ  Type of Shell: /bin/bash                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Your main concern is to "crack" each encrypted password for every     บ
 บ  user.  Because the encryption function is only unidirectional, you        บ
 บ  cannot decrypt the encrypted password.  You must run a "cracking"         บ
 บ  program which encrypts words and then compares the encrypted word with    บ
 บ  the password.  If they match, you have now "cracked" the password.        บ
 บ  Because cracking relies on words that are encrypted, you MUST have a      บ
 บ  wordlist.  For beginners a basic wordlist can be found as a dictionary    บ
 บ  file supplied as a part of UNIX.  The more comprehensive the wordlist     บ
 บ  is, the better your chances of successfully cracking passwords.  Next     บ
 บ  you'll need a "passwd" cracker, which can be found in versions made for   บ
 บ  UNIX & DOS.  The best DOS cracker is currently CrackerJack and the best   บ
 บ  UNIX cracker is currently Crack.  Next, run the "cracking" program and    บ
 บ  feed it your wordlist and passwd file, and watch as it "cracks" the       บ
 บ  passwords.                                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Sometimes you'll discover that the "passwd" file is incomplete or     บ
 บ  looks something like this :                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  bgates:*:5604:12:William Gates:/home/bgates:/bin/bash                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The * is called the token and means that the passwd file has been     บ
 บ  shadowed.  Password shadowing is a security system where the encrypted    บ
 บ  password field of /etc/passwd is replaced with a special token and the    บ
 บ  encrypted password is stored in a separate file which is not readable by  บ
 บ  normal system users. In order to defeat this, you'll need to write a C    บ
 บ  program and compile it similar to this :                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  -------Sample UnShadow Program------------------------------------------  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  #include <pwd.h>                                                          บ
 บ  main()                                                                    บ
 บ  {                                                                         บ
 บ  struct passwd *p;                                                         บ
 บ  while(p=getpwent())                                                       บ
 บ  printf("%s:%s:%d:%d:%s:%s:%s\n", p->pw_name, p->pw_passwd,                บ
 บ  p->pw_uid, p->pw_gid, p->pw_gecos, p->pw_dir, p->pw_shell);               บ
 บ  }                                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  -------End of Sample Program--------------------------------------------  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The "passwd" file is located in the following pathes for each         บ
 บ  system.  To determine your UNIX system type, enter the following during   บ
 บ  the UNIX prompt :                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  uname -a                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  UNIX Paths (Courtesy of 2600)                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  UNIX                  Path                            Token               บ
 บ  -----------------------------------------------------------------         บ
 บ  AIX 3                 /etc/security/passwd            !                   บ
 บ         or             /tcb/auth/files/<first letter   #                   บ
 บ                              of username>/<username>                       บ
 บ  A/UX 3.0s             /tcb/files/auth/?/*                                 บ
 บ  BSD4.3-Reno           /etc/master.passwd              *                   บ
 บ  ConvexOS 10           /etc/shadpw                     *                   บ
 บ  ConvexOS 11           /etc/shadow                     *                   บ
 บ  DG/UX                 /etc/tcb/aa/user/               *                   บ
 บ  EP/IX                 /etc/shadow                     x                   บ
 บ  HP-UX                 /.secure/etc/passwd             *                   บ
 บ  IRIX 5                /etc/shadow                     x                   บ
 บ  Linux 1.1             /etc/shadow                     *                   บ
 บ  OSF/1                 /etc/passwd[.dir|.pag]          *                   บ
 บ  SCO Unix #.2.x        /tcb/auth/files/<first letter   *                   บ
 บ                               of username>/<username>                      บ
 บ  SunOS4.1+c2           /etc/security/passwd.adjunct    ##username          บ
 บ  SunOS 5.0             /etc/shadow                                         บ
 บ                        <optional NIS+ private secure maps/tables>          บ
 บ  System V Release 4.0  /etc/shadow                     x                   บ
 บ  System V Release 4.2  /etc/security/* database                            บ
 บ  Ultrix 4              /etc/auth[.dir|.pag]            *                   บ
 บ  UNICOS                /etc/udb                        *                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  (This TEXT is for informational purposes only)                            บ

 บ    Author  : Crystaline Death                                              บ
 บ    Subject : "Me... a Narq?"                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      We all know about the groups that release cool warez and all that     บ
 บ  good shit.  But did you know there are like a lot of groups popping up    บ
 บ  all over the fucking place?  I am not saying that this isn't good or      บ
 บ  anything, but why?  It seems that most of the groups that start out (and  บ
 บ  survive) merge.  And after a while, the merged group merges with another  บ
 บ  group.  Eventually, that group merges with a group like DOD or            บ
 บ  something.  It always ends up with big groups and on the way there,       บ
 บ  during merging, people have to be cut!  I was in groups such as Imperial  บ
 บ  and Siva, where one day, they would merge, and then the next day, it      บ
 บ  would have been like the whole thing never happened.                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Being a mere coder, I just can't keep up with the 0 hour shit, but I  บ
 บ  try as hard as I can.  Anyways, I was afraid I was going to be cut (I     บ
 บ  don't know why, Zorlac is a cool dude.).  But anyways, when Imperial      บ
 บ  merged, they didn't cut many people.  However, a few days before they     บ
 บ  merged, 2 people came up to me (Trite and MGD) and informed me that       บ
 บ  Imperial was most likely going to merge and everyone in Imperial would    บ
 บ  get screwed except Trite, Zorlac and the suppliers of Imperial.  This     บ
 บ  got me a bit worried, so I asked everyone that would possibly get cut to  บ
 บ  write a text file with their information in it. (email address, handle,   บ
 บ  and position in Imperial), so I left it at that.                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The next day, I come into #Imperial to say my daily greets to people  บ
 บ  I know.  In a matter of seconds, Zorlac started to curse me off because   บ
 บ  I had been accused of trying to steal Imperial members into joining       บ
 บ  Siva.  I was then kicked and banned.  My response was "What the hell is   บ
 บ  going on?"  So I chatted around to find out what happened.  Apparently,   บ
 บ  someone was out to get me bad.  I was informed by Hybernate that someone  บ
 บ  using my handle went into #Imperial and told everyone to join Siva and    บ
 บ  to fuck Imperial.  I personally didn't know at the time who it was, but   บ
 บ  I could only think that Trite or MGD might have done it.  When I told     บ
 บ  Zorlac (after he calmed down thanks to Forseer) that Trite and MGD told   บ
 บ  me about the merge, he went to Trite and asked him about this.  Trite     บ
 บ  told zorlac that he didn't say shit to me (he was lying).  So, the only   บ
 บ  logical thing was that Trite was the one trying to fuck me over.          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Eventually, with the help of personality witnesses (I am usually a    บ
 บ  joker, or quite senile) they got me back into Imperial, but it was        บ
 บ  really Forseer who bailed me out.  He told me that he got me out of hot   บ
 บ  water with Zorlac and that I would be considered innocent until they      บ
 บ  checked out the bot logs.  A few days later, the whole thing blew down.   บ
 บ  No one accused me of anything, for which I am quite pleased.              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Personal Greets Go Out To :                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Forseer : Dude, thanks a lot for bailing me out!  If it wasn't for you,   บ
 บ            who knows what would have happened.  If you need anything at    บ
 บ            all, you know where to find me, #Imperial, #Siva, #FDM, and     บ
 บ            #RCN.                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Zorlac  : Yeah, I was pissed at you for the shortest of times Zorlac,     บ
 บ            but I knew I could convince you that I didn't do it.  Thanks a  บ
 บ            lot for listening and always being there.  Zorlac, you are one  บ
 บ            of the few Presidents I know that care.                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Hectic  : Thanks a lot for the t3 Netcom shell and for hooking me up      บ
 บ            with the warez!                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  X-Factor, Infinite, and Hybernate : Thanks for sticking up for me and     บ
 บ                                      being personality witnesses.  See     บ
 บ                                      you all on IRC!                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Yeah yeah, this article might have cost you 5 minutes of your         บ
 บ  precious time, but someday, you will all thank me!                        บ

 บ    Author  : Tuxedo Mask                                                   บ
 บ    Subject : $60 for this?                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Every game player has lived through this scenario in one form or      บ
 บ  another : shell out $60 for a game, then after 15 minutes of playing it   บ
 บ  at home, you realize that it stinks.  As you stare at the piece of        บ
 บ  plastic software nestled in your system, you ask, "Why did I have to pay  บ
 บ  $60 for this?  At this price, am I getting a fair shake here?  After      บ
 บ  all, older games sell for as low as $10, but aren't much different from   บ
 บ  the $60 games."                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      These concerns are shared by many, especially in today's era of CD    บ
 บ  games that don't differ materially from music CDs but cost four times as  บ
 บ  much.  What are people paying for when they decide to shell out their     บ
 บ  dough for games?  An exact answer remains elusive, as every game takes    บ
 บ  shape under different development and marketing budgets.  Plus,           บ
 บ  companies try to keep such data out of public realm for business          บ
 บ  reasons.                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      After talking to a few PC Game developers (I keep in touch with a     บ
 บ  few local programmers, industry officials, and market analysts), I've     บ
 บ  pieced together a general picture of what gamers pay to play, as shown    บ
 บ  on the charts at the bottom of the article.                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      In theory, only two things matter to gamers : someone to program the  บ
 บ  game and the parts needed to build it.  On average, only $7 to $10 of a   บ
 บ  game's worth goes toward the actual programming and debugging.  Add to    บ
 บ  that the cost to "build" one game - about $5 for a CD - and the sum       บ
 บ  comprises merely $12-$15 of a game's price tag.                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      So why pay more?  In reality, the pricing breakdown for a specific    บ
 บ  game has more variables than any algebra test.  Some factors weigh more   บ
 บ  heavily than others.  Between 10 and 15 percent of your cash goes back    บ
 บ  to the company that created the operating system which your game will be  บ
 บ  running on.  Think of it as a "tax" that publishers must pay for the      บ
 บ  right to sell games which require DOS, Win95, OS/2, etc.  That "tax" is   บ
 บ  directly tacked onto the cost of the game.  However, individual           บ
 บ  publishers almost always craft deals to reduce these fees.                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Does the game have ties to a hit movie, or sports license from both   บ
 บ  the players and the league or is sanctioned by a superstar?  If so,       บ
 บ  it'll jack up the cost of a game.  According to my sources, the costs of  บ
 บ  acquiring such rights can account for up to 20 percent or more of a       บ
 บ  game's price tag.  There's one fee of 15 percent for a player's license   บ
 บ  and another separate fee for a league license.  In all sports except the  บ
 บ  NBA, the licenses have to be negotiated separately.  In most cases,       บ
 บ  costs range from $3-5 for movie ties and $8-10 for one sports license     บ
 บ  and double that for baseball and football titles.                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Remember the TV ad that prompted you to get that fighting game?       บ
 บ  Well, you helped pay for the ad when you bought the game.  Also, roughly  บ
 บ  20 percent of a game's price comes from retail markup.  However, none of  บ
 บ  this really matters since anyone reading this probably pirates a large    บ
 บ  percent of the games they play.  Again, according to my sources,          บ
 บ  game companies also have to account for what they COULD have made if      บ
 บ  PC games were not so widely pirated.  What does that mean?  Well,         บ
 บ  companies jack up the prices of their products by up to 20 percent in     บ
 บ  order to account for their losses caused by pirates.  So the next time    บ
 บ  you're downloading a game, whether it's off of a BBS or a FTP site,       บ
 บ  remember, somebody's paying for your piracy...                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      This rivalry could very well have a lot to do with Intel FINALLY      บ
 บ  making dramatic price cuts on the Pentium prices.  Naturally, they        บ
 บ  screwed us as long as they could, but now that Cyrix has begun MASS       บ
 บ  production of their TESTED (unlike Intel) CPUs, Intel has good reason to  บ
 บ  worry that the millions of LAMERS might notice the severe price           บ
 บ  difference of products.  The Cyrix 6x86-100 Mhz CPU cost $450/ea in       บ
 บ  stocks of 1,000, while the rival Intel Pentium 133 Mhz CPU is a much      บ
 บ  higher $520/ea in stocks of 1,000.                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Cyrix has pushed their efforts to create a superior CPU ahead of the  บ
 บ  Pentium age.  I believe they have succeeded.  It's time that people rely  บ
 บ  more on their own research when they purchase products such as CPUs and   บ
 บ  other computer related products.  It's important to know how your         บ
 บ  computer functions, but more important to know it functions at its        บ
 บ  highest capabilities for your hard earned dollar.                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 บ  ภฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤู  บ

 บ                                                                            บ

 บ                                                                            บ

 บ                                                                            บ

 บ                                                                            บ

 บ                                                                            บ

 บ                               movie or sports league ties such as the      บ
 บ                               NBA, NFL, or NHL)                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ                                                                            บ

 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Games                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the five best games release groups in the        บ
 บ  scene.  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will  บ
 บ  be!  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but    บ
 บ  you will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's  บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The game didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The game was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  util will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Games                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the five best games release groups in the        บ
 บ  scene.  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will  บ
 บ  be!  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but    บ
 บ  you will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's  บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The game didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The game was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  util will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Games Reviewed : 04/25/96 -> 05/01/96            ณ  บ
 บ  ภฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤู  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Games                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the five best games release groups in the        บ
 บ  scene.  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will  บ
 บ  be!  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but    บ
 บ  you will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's  บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The game didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The game was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  util will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Games Reviewed : 05/02/96 -> 05/08/96            ณ  บ
 บ  ภฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤู  บ

                                         ฿     r e v i e w s !

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Games                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the five best games release groups in the        บ
 บ  scene.  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will  บ
 บ  be!  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but    บ
 บ  you will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's  บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The game didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The game was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  util will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Games Reviewed : 05/09/96 -> 05/15/96            ณ  บ
 บ  ภฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤู  บ

 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Utils                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the five best utils release groups in the        บ
 บ  scene.  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will  บ
 บ  be!  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but    บ
 บ  you will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's  บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The util didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The util was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  util will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Utils Reviewed : 04/18/96 -> 04/24/96            ณ  บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Utils                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the five best utils release groups in the        บ
 บ  scene.  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will  บ
 บ  be!  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but    บ
 บ  you will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's  บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The util didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The util was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  util will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Utils Reviewed : 04/25/96 -> 05/01/96            ณ  บ
 บ  ภฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤู  บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Utils                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the five best utils release groups in the        บ
 บ  scene.  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will  บ
 บ  be!  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but    บ
 บ  you will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's  บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The util didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The util was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  util will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Utils Reviewed : 05/02/96 -> 05/08/96            ณ  บ
 บ  ภฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤู  บ
