 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Utils                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the five best utils release groups in the        บ
 บ  scene.  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will  บ
 บ  be!  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but    บ
 บ  you will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's  บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The util didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The util was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  util will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Utils Reviewed : 05/09/96 -> 05/15/96            ณ  บ
 บ  ภฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤู  บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Welcome to Dear Road Rebel!  This is going to be YOUR column that is  บ
 บ  a cross between Dear Abby and Dave Berry.  The most important part of     บ
 บ  this is YOUR participation.  If you have ever had a question about the    บ
 บ  scene or just a comment, here's the place!  Have you ever wanted to know  บ
 บ  why some people do this or that?  ASK!  I would love to take it to the    บ
 บ  extreme for you and we will be happy to research it!  I hope you have as  บ
 บ  much fun with this as I will!  Remember, this is YOUR column!             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Topic For Next Week : The Internet and the BBS scene.                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The Internet was introduced to us just a few years ago.  In reality,  บ
 บ  it is a relatively new resource for us all.  Yet it has managed to take   บ
 บ  the scene by surprise and is now an indepensible resource that we could   บ
 บ  not manage without.  Previous to the Internet, BBSs were the only method  บ
 บ  of warez transport.  Couriers had to work hard to get a release from      บ
 บ  one board to all the rest, a feat that is rather amazing to me today      บ
 บ  when I look back.  However, with the advent of the Internet, a file can   บ
 บ  make it around the world in under 5 minutes!  Most files reach the top    บ
 บ  boards within 6 hours of their release!  Still, though, BBSs do have      บ
 บ  clear advantages over the Internet.  Some of these advantages are a       บ
 บ  searchable file base, easier access restriction, and most of all, a       บ
 บ  public message base, one that, on the Internet, could only be controlled  บ
 บ  through a fast listserv.  Why haven't all these T1 FTP sites converted    บ
 บ  to telnet nodes for a PCBoard setup?  What do you think the Internet has  บ
 บ  done to the BBS scene?  What do you think the BBS scene will be like in   บ
 บ  a year or two?  What do you think the Internet will be like then?  How    บ
 บ  do you feel about this technological revolution?                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน

 บ      Test your knowledge of the WAREZ SCENE!  The following are TEN mind   บ
 บ  boggling "YOU DON'T KNOW NOTHIN'" questions!  Enter all your answers in,  บ
 บ  and when you feel you're happy with them, press F10 and the computer      บ
 บ  will tally up your score and spit it out at you.  For every question you  บ
 บ  missed, the computer will indicate the correct answer.  Oh, and if you    บ
 บ  feel like "You Don't Know Nothin'" midway through the quiz and don't      บ
 บ  want to embarrass yourself with an incredibly low score, press ESC and    บ
 บ  you'll be back on the bright side of RCN, the awesome music will calm     บ
 บ  you down, and all will be well again.. enjoy!                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  *PS* All answers are found in back issues of RCN!                         บ
